\section{External states: ${e_{{i}}, \bar{e}_{{j}}, u_{{k}}, \bar{u}_{{l}}}$} 
\subsection{Wave contributions, Propagator: $A^0$} 



 \begin{center}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{\eta_i}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{\eta_i}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,R}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{b, i} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{c, b} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W^+}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W^+}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLL= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^-,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^-,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRR= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^-,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^-,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRL= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^-,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^-,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLR= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^-,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^-,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^+ ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSOlluuVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{H^-_{{b}}}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{H^-_{{b}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^- ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^+,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLL= & 0 \\

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{h_{{a}}}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{h_{{a}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{u}u A^0 ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{A^0}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\

  PSOlluuSLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{u}u \eta_i ,R}_{c, k} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e \eta_i ,L}_{j, i} \frac{1}{m^2_{\eta_i}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{u}d H^- ,R}_{l, b, a} \Gamma^{\bar{d}u H^+,L}_{b, c, a} I_2 m^2_{u_{{l}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{u}d H^- ,L}_{l, b, a} \Gamma^{\bar{d}u H^+,L}_{b, c, a} I_1 m_{u_{{l}}} m_{d_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{u}d H^- ,L}_{l, b, a} \Gamma^{\bar{d}u H^+,R}_{b, c, a} I_2 m_{u_{{l}}} m_{u_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{u}d H^- ,R}_{l, b, a} \Gamma^{\bar{d}u H^+,R}_{b, c, a} I_1 m_{d_{{b}}} m_{u_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{u_{{l}}} - m^2_{u_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSOlluuVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuVLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSOlluuTLL= & 0 \\
